<header id="article-header_1-0" class="comp right-rail__offset js-toc-appear article-header mntl-block">
<h1 id="article-heading_2-0" class="comp article-heading mntl-text-block">
The 10 Richest People in the World</h1>
<div id="sponsorship-wrapper_1-0" class="comp sponsorship-wrapper mntl-block"></div>
<div id="article-meta_1-0" class="comp article-meta mntl-block" data-tracking-container="true">
<div id="finance-bylines_1-0" class="comp finance-bylines mntl-bylines">
<div id="mntl-bylines__group_1-0" class="comp mntl-bylines__group--author mntl-bylines__group mntl-block">
<div id="mntl-bylines__item_1-0" class="comp mntl-bylines__item mntl-attribution__item mntl-attribution__item--has-date">
<span class="mntl-attribution__item-descriptor">By</span>
<div data-tooltip="Dan Moskowitz is a freelance financial writer who has 4&#43; years of experience creating content for the online reading market." data-inline-tooltip="true">
<a
href="https://www.investopedia.com/contributors/53695/"
rel="nocaes"
data-trigger-link="true"
class="mntl-attribution__item-name"
>Dan Moskowitz</a>
<div id="mntl-author-tooltip_1-0" class="comp mntl-author-tooltip mntl-tooltip mntl-group">
<div class="mntl-author-tooltip__top ">
<div class="mntl-author-tooltip__image-wrapper">

</header>
</div>
<div class="loc article-content">
<div id="article-body_1-0" class="comp article-body mntl-block" data-contain-tooltips="true">
<div id="mntl-sc-page_1-0" class="comp article-body-content mntl-sc-page mntl-block" data-sc-sticky-offset="80" data-sc-ad-label-height="0" data-sc-ad-track-spacing="90" data-sc-min-track-height="250" data-sc-max-track-height="600" data-sc-breakpoint="50em" data-sc-load-immediate="2" data-sc-content-positions="[300, 1, 1, 1250, 1, 1, 1, 1]" data-bind-scroll-on-start="true">
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Billionaires play an outsized role in shaping the global economy, politics, and philanthropy. Forbes puts the number of billionaires in the world at 2,668 in 2022. The wealthiest among them is (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=lvmh" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">LVMH</a>) co-founder and chief executive officer (CEO) Bernard Arnault, who became the richest man in the world in 2022.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="278"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="238"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-1" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-2" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
The individuals on this list belong to an even more exclusive club and wield still more power. Many are founders of technology giants, with much of their wealth still invested in the companies they started.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-3" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-4" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
These billionaires can, however, still borrow against that wealth to avoid selling stock, deferring (or eliminating for heirs) taxes on <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/u/unrealizedgain.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">unrealized capital gains</a> in the process. Multi-billionaires can also take advantage of a panoply of tax deductions to offset reported income, leaving some on this list paying no income tax in recent years.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="205"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="206"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-5" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-6" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
With so much of their wealth in publicly traded stocks, the net worth of the richest can fluctuate with market valuations. For example, Tesla CEO Elon Musk saw his <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/n/networth.asp" class="pseudoStyle" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">net worth</a> surge in 2021 thanks to the increase in the electric car maker's share price. Tesla shares rose nearly 50% in 2021. And like a pendulum, his net worth dropped in 2022 due to the falling share price of Tesla, of which he owns 13%. Musk also had to sell many of his shares in Tesla to fund his acquisition of Twitter. As of February 16, 2023, Tesla stock closed at $202.04, more than half of the $409.97 share price in November 2021. In December 2022, Musk lost the title of the richest person in the world to Arnault.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="191"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="278"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="181"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-7" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-8" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Similarly, Meta Platforms (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=META" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">META</a>) founder and CEO Mark Zuckerberg fell out of the top 10 in February 2022, when the company's share price plunged after a disappointing earnings report. Zuckerberg's net worth was reported to be $53.1 billion in January 2023.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="234"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-9" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-10" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Below are the 10 wealthiest people on the planet, according to the Bloomberg Billionaires Index. All figures are current as of Jan. 26, 2023, unless otherwise stated.<br/>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-11" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-12" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-callout mntl-block">
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-13" class="comp theme-whatyouneedtoknow mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-callout mntl-block" data-tracking-id="mntl-sc-block-callout" data-tracking-container="true">
<h3 id="mntl-sc-block-callout-heading_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-heading mntl-text-block">
Key Takeaways</h3>
<div id="mntl-sc-block-callout-body_1-0" class="comp mntl-sc-block-callout-body mntl-text-block">
<ul><li>Bernard Arnault, co-founder, chair, and CEO of LVMH, is the richest person and the richest man in the world with a net worth of $190 billion.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="278"></span></li><li>After Arnault is co-founder and CEO of Tesla, Elon Musk.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="278"></span></li><li>Other billionaires with some of the largest net worths include India&#39;s Gautam Adani, Amazon founder Jeff Bezos, and Microsoft&#39;s Bill Gates.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span></li><li>Six of the top 10 billionaires made their fortunes in technology, with Arnault, Berkshire Hathaway&#39;s Warren Buffett, Adani Group founder Gautam Adani, and America Movil&#39;s Carlos Slim being the exceptions.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span></li><li>Meta&#39;s Mark Zuckerberg dropped off the top 10 list in February 2022.</li></ul></div>
</div>
</div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-1-bernard-arnault"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-14" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 1. Bernard Arnault </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-15" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age:</strong> 73</li>
<li><strong>Residence:</strong> Paris</li>
<li><strong>CEO and Chair:</strong> LVMH (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=LVMUY" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">LVMUY</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Net Worth: </strong>$190 billion</li>
<li><strong>Christian Dior Ownership Stake:</strong> 97.5% ($151 billion total)</li>
<li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> Moelis &amp; Company equity ($28.6 billion public asset) and $11 billion in cash<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="166"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-16" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-17" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
French national&nbsp;<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/b/bernard-arnault.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Bernard Arnault</a>&nbsp;is the chair and CEO of LVMH, the world’s largest luxury goods company. LVMH brands include&nbsp;Louis Vuitton, Hennessey, Marc Jacobs, and Sephora.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="45"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-18" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-19" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Most of Arnault's wealth comes from his massive stake in Christian Dior SE, the <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/h/holdingcompany.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">holding company</a> that controls 41.2% of LVMH. His shares in Christian Dior SE, plus an additional 6.2% in LVMH, are held through his family-owned holding company, Groupe Familial Arnault.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="166"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-20" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-21" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.6%;">
<img
data-src="https://www.investopedia.com/thmb/HVyDj10f_aq5aqo3RVfclshCCso=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/GettyImages-696695914-895a5475a7f8412c9239900be0ea5179.jpg"

</noscript>
</div>
</div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Christophe Morin / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-22" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
An engineer by training, Arnault first showed his business acumen while working for his father’s construction firm, Ferret-Savinel, taking charge of the company in 1971. He converted Ferret-Savinel to a real estate company named Férinel Inc. in 1979.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="47"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-23" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-24" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Arnault remained Férinel&#39;s chair for another six years, until he acquired and reorganized luxury goods maker Financière Agache in 1984, eventually selling all its holdings other than Christian Dior and Le Bon Marché. He was invited to invest in LVMH in 1987 and became the majority shareholder, chair of the board, and CEO of the company two years later.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="49"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="143"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-25" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-2-elon-musk"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-26" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 2. Elon Musk </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-27" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age:</strong> 51</li><li><strong>Residence:</strong> Texas</li><li><strong>Co-founder and CEO:</strong> Tesla</li><li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $146 billion</li><li><strong>Tesla Ownership Stake:</strong> 13% ($51.5 billion)</li><li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> Space Exploration Technologies ($48.9 billion private asset), The Boring Company ($3.33 billion private asset), Twitter ($11.6 billion private asset)<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="181"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-28" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-29" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/articles/personal-finance/061015/how-elon-musk-became-elon-musk.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Elon Musk</a> is the second-richest man in the world. He was born in South Africa and attended a university in Canada before transferring to the University of Pennsylvania, where he earned bachelor's degrees in physics and economics. Two days after enrolling in a graduate physics program at Stanford University, Musk deferred attendance to launch Zip2, one of the earliest online navigation services. He reinvested a portion of the proceeds from this startup to create X.com, the online payment system that was sold to eBay (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=ebay" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="2">EBAY</a>) and ultimately became PayPal Holdings (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=pypl" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="3">PYPL</a>).<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="209"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-30" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-31" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
In 2004, Musk became a major funder of Tesla Motors (now Tesla), which led to his current position as CEO of the electric vehicle company. In addition to its line of electric automobiles, Tesla produces energy storage devices, automobile accessories, and, through its <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/a/acquisition.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">acquisition</a> of SolarCity in 2016, solar power systems. Musk is also CEO and chief engineer of Space Exploration Technologies (SpaceX), a developer of space launch rockets.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="197"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="141"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="209"></span><br>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-32" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-33" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
In 2020, Tesla shares soared 740% to propel Musk up the wealth rankings. In December 2020, Tesla joined the <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/s/sp500.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">S&amp;P 500</a>, becoming the largest company added. In January 2021, Musk became the richest person in the world—a title he held till December 2022, when his net worth fell due to a decrease in Tesla's share price over the year.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="181"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="278"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="195"></span><br>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-34" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-35" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.6%;">
<img
data-src="https://www.investopedia.com/thmb/uelBHQSMMMuACDanqT2SYCQWIXU=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/GettyImages-1215628293-c32a14bc41c34aa9adee9e41f6c7fb68.jpg"
width="5760"
height="3840"
data-srcset="https://www.investopedia.com/thmb/LupBrpXSGSitw4cCciFeCUgewsM=/750x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/GettyImages-1215628293-c32a14bc41c34aa9adee9e41f6c7fb68.jpg 750w"
data-sizes="750px"
alt="Elon Musk"

<noscript>

</noscript>
</div>
</div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-1" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Saul Martinez / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-36" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Musk asked his Twitter audience on Nov. 6, 2021, whether he should sell 10% of his Tesla stock, framing the issue as a response to criticism of unrealized capital gains as a means of avoiding taxes. He proceeded to sell shares worth $16.4 billion over the remainder of 2021.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="210"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="211"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-37" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-38" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
U.S. Sen. Elizabeth Warren, a Massachusetts Democrat, cited a media report that Musk paid no income tax for 2018 to argue for the adoption of a wealth tax. &#34;And if you opened your eyes for two seconds, you would realize I will pay more taxes than any American in history this year,&#34; Musk responded on Twitter.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="212"></span><br/>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-39" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-40" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Thanks to the surge in Tesla shares in 2021 and private transactions boosting the reported valuation of SpaceX, Musk&#39;s lead in the global wealth rankings continued to grow. His net worth hit a high of $340 billion in November 2021.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-41" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-42" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
In April 2022, <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/musk-bids-to-take-twitter-private-5225910" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Musk began a campaign to take Twitter private</a>, which culminated in a $44 billion buyout. Musk planned to fund the deal with $21 billion of his own capital. In the run-up to the buyout announcement, Musk sold 9.6 million shares of Tesla, valued at roughly $8.5 billion.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="252"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="251"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-43" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-44" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
In July 2022, Musk decided to back out of the Twitter buyout. Twitter filed a lawsuit against Musk to force the buyout to go through. Musk countersued the company but then reversed course and declared he was willing to buy Twitter after all. The deal officially closed in October 2022, giving him an almost 80% stake in the company.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="268"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="253"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-45" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-3-jeff-bezos"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-46" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 3. Jeff Bezos </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-47" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age:</strong> 58</li>
<li><strong>Residence:</strong> Washington</li>
<li><strong>Founder and Executive Chair:</strong> Amazon (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=amzn" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">AMZN</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $120 billion</li>
<li><strong>Amazon Ownership Stake: </strong>10% ($96.5 billion)</li>
<li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> Blue Origin ($9.15 billion private asset), <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/billionaires-who-bought-publishers-5270187" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="2">The Washington Post</a> ($250 million private asset), and $14.6 billion in cash<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="169"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-48" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-49" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
In 1994,&nbsp;<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/investing/how-jeff-bezos-got-be-worlds-richest-man/" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Jeff Bezos</a>&nbsp;founded&nbsp;Amazon.com in a garage in Seattle, shortly after he resigned from the hedge fund giant D.E. Shaw. He had originally pitched the idea of an online bookstore&nbsp;to his former boss David E. Shaw, who wasn’t interested.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="24"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="25"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-50" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-51" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Though Amazon&nbsp;originally started out selling books, it has since morphed into a one-stop shop for everything under the sun and&nbsp;is expected to overtake Walmart as the world’s largest retailer by 2024. Amazon's pattern of constant <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/d/diversification.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">diversification</a> is evident in some of its&nbsp;unexpected expansions, which include acquiring Whole Foods&nbsp;in 2017 and entering the pharmacy business the same year.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="134"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="28"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-52" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-53" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.6%;">
<img
data-src="https://www.investopedia.com/thmb/Md63PXpeOkYry4OJqetJOEapANw=/1500x0/filters:no_upscale():max_bytes(150000):strip_icc():format(webp)/GettyImages-1036094130-cf8da629f9b44c81a0b1398311ac5787.jpg"

</noscript>
</div>
</div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-2" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Alex Wong / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-54" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Bezos owned as much as 16% of Amazon in 2019 before transferring 4% to his former wife, MacKenzie Scott, as part of their divorce proceedings. In 2020, Amazon’s share price jumped 76% on the heightened demand for online shopping amid the COVID-19 <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/special-economic-impact-of-pandemics-4800597" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">pandemic</a>. On July 5, 2021, Bezos stepped down as CEO of the <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/e/ecommerce.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="2">e-commerce</a> giant, becoming its executive chair.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="169"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="132"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-55" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-56" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Bezos originally took Amazon public in 1997 and went on to become the first man since Bill Gates in 1999 to achieve a net worth of more than $100 billion. Bezos’ other projects include aerospace company Blue Origin, <em>The Washington Post </em>(which he purchased in 2013), and the 10,000-year clock—also known as the Long Now.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="184"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="186"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="185"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-57" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-58" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
On July 20, 2021, Bezos, his brother Mark, aviation pioneer Wally Funk, and Dutch student Oliver Daemen completed Blue Origin&#39;s first successful crewed flight, reaching an altitude of more than 66 miles before landing safely. Bezos&#39; wealth peaked at $211 billion in the same month.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="169"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="196"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="187"></span><br/>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-59" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-4-gautam-adani"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-60" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 4. Gautam Adani </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-61" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age: </strong>60</li><li><strong>Residence: </strong>Gurgaon, India</li><li><strong>Founder and Chair: </strong>Adani Group</li><li><strong>Net Worth: </strong>$113 billion</li><li><strong>Adani Enterprises, Adani Power, and Adani Transmissions Ownership Stakes: </strong>75% each ($64.24 billion)</li><li><strong>Other Assets: </strong>66% of Adani Ports &amp; Special Economic Zone ($10 billion public asset), 61% of Adani Green Energy ($21 billion public asset), 37% of Adani Total Gas ($18.5 billion public asset)<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="220"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-62" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-63" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Gautam Adani, the founder of Adani Group, surpassed Mukesh Ambani in March 2022 as the richest person in Asia. Through his ownership of the Adani Group, Adani owns major stakes in six key Indian companies, including a 75% stake in Adani Enterprises, Adani Power, and Adani Transmissions, as well as a 66% stake in Adani Ports &amp; Special Economic Zone, 61% stake in Adani Green Energy, and a 37% stake in Adani Total Gas.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="220"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-64" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-65" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">

<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-3" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Dipam Bhachech / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-66" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Adani entered the power generation market in 2009 with Adani Power. Adani created Adani Enterprises in 1988 to import and export <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/c/commodity.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">commodities</a>. In 1994, his company was granted approval to develop a harbor facility at Mundra Port, which is now the largest private port in India.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="236"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="220"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-67" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-68" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Adani dropped out of college and previously worked in the diamond trade. Adani now has the largest port operator, closely-held thermal coal producer, and coal trader in India. In 2020, he purchased a 74% stake in Mumbai&#39;s Chhatrapati Shivaji International Airport, India&#39;s second-busiest airport.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-69" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-70" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
The billionaire was kidnapped and held for ransom in 1997. Adani was also in Mumbai’s Taj hotel during the 2008 terrorist attack.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="237"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="220"></span><br/>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-71" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-5-bill-gates"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-72" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 5. Bill Gates </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-73" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age:</strong> 67</li>
<li><strong>Residence:</strong> Washington</li>
<li><strong>Co-founder: </strong>Microsoft (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=msft" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">MSFT</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $111 billion</li>
<li><strong>Microsoft</strong> <strong>Ownership Stake: </strong>1.4% ($24.8 billion)</li>
<li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> $57.2 billion in cash and billions over multiple other companies<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="208"></span><br><br></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-74" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-75" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
While attending Harvard University in 1975, <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/articles/markets/101215/what-bill-gatess-portfolio-looks.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Bill Gates</a> went to work alongside his childhood friend Paul Allen to develop new software for the original microcomputers. Following this project’s success, Gates dropped out of Harvard during his junior year and founded Microsoft with Allen.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="33"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="144"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-76" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-77" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
The largest software company in the world, Microsoft, also produces a line of personal computers, provides email services through its exchange server, and sells video game systems and associated game devices. It has recently invested heavily in cloud services.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="36"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="199"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-78" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-79" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Gates shifted from the company&#39;s CEO to the role of board chair in 2008. He joined Berkshire Hathaway’s board in 2004. He stepped down from both boards on March 13, 2020.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="38"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="13"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="213"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-80" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-81" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">

</div>
</div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-4" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Jack Taylor / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-82" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Bill Gates has much of his net worth in <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/articles/personal-finance/111214/where-does-bill-gates-keep-his-money.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Cascade Investment LLC</a>. Cascade is a privately-held investment vehicle that owns a variety of stocks including Canadian National Railway (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=CNR" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="2">CNR</a>), Deere (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=DE" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="3">DE</a>), and Republic Services (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=RSG" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="4">RSG</a>), as well as private investments in real estate and energy.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="208"></span><br>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-83" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-6-warren-buffett"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-84" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 6. Warren Buffett </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-85" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age: </strong>92</li>
<li><strong>Residence:</strong> Nebraska</li>
<li><strong>CEO:</strong> Berkshire Hathaway (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=BRK.A" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">BRK.A</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $108 billion</li>
<li><strong>Berkshire Hathaway Ownership Stake:</strong> 14% ($107 billion)</li>
<li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> $1.13 billion in cash<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="172"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-86" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-87" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
The most famous living value investor, <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/articles/01/071801.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Warren Buffett</a> filed his first tax return in 1944 at age 14, declaring earnings from his boyhood paper route. He first bought shares in a textile company called Berkshire Hathaway in 1962, becoming the majority shareholder by 1965. Buffett expanded the company's holdings to insurance and other investments in 1967.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="86"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-88" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-89" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Widely known as the Oracle of Omaha, Buffett is a buy-and-hold investor who built his fortune by acquiring <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/u/undervalued.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">undervalued</a> companies. More recently, Berkshire Hathaway has invested in large, well-known companies. Its portfolio of wholly owned subsidiaries includes interests in insurance, energy distribution, and railroads as well as consumer products.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="150"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="214"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="88"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-90" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-91" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Buffett is a notable Bitcoin skeptic.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="137"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-92" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-93" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:70.0%;">

<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-5" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Alex Wong / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-94" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Buffett has dedicated much of his wealth to philanthropy. Between 2006 and 2020, he gave away $41 billion—mostly to the Bill &amp; Melinda Gates Foundation and his children’s charities. Buffett launched the Giving Pledge alongside Bill Gates in 2010.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="156"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="93"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-95" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-96" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Now 92 years old, Buffett still serves as CEO, but in 2021 he hinted that his successor might be Gregory Abel, head of Berkshire’s non-insurance operations.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-97" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-7-larry-ellison"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-98" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 7. Larry Ellison </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-99" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age:</strong> 78</li>
<li><strong>Residence:</strong> Hawaii</li>
<li><strong>Co-founder, Chair, and CTO:</strong> Oracle (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=ORCL" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">ORCL</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $100 billion</li>
<li><strong>Oracle Ownership Stake:</strong> 40%+ ($75.2 billion)</li>
<li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> Tesla equity ($6.5 billion public asset), $18 billion in cash<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="269"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-100" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-101" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/l/larry-ellison.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Larry Ellison</a> was born in New York City to a 19-year-old single mother. After dropping out of the University of Chicago in 1966, Ellison moved to California and worked as a computer programmer. In 1973, he joined the electronics company Ampex, where he met future partners Ed Oates and Bob Miner. Three years later, Ellison moved to Precision Instruments, serving as the company’s vice president of research and development.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="274"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-102" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-103" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
In 1977, Ellison founded Software Development Laboratories alongside Oates and Miner. Two years later, the company released Oracle, the first commercial relational database program to use Structured Query Language. The database program proved so popular that SDL would change its name to Oracle Systems Corporation in 1982. Ellison gave up the CEO role at Oracle in 2014 after 37 years. He joined Tesla&#39;s board in December 2018 and stepped down in June 2022.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="270"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="271"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="272"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-104" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-105" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Oracle is the world&#39;s second-largest software company, providing a wide variety of cloud computing programs as well as Java and Linux code and the Oracle Exadata computing platform.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-106" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-107" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Oracle has acquired numerous large companies, including human resources management systems provider PeopleSoft in 2005, customer relationship management applications provider Siebel in 2006, enterprise infrastructure software provider BEA Systems in 2008, and hardware-and-software developer Sun Microsystems in 2009. In December 2021, Oracle agreed to buy medical records software provider Cerner (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=cern" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">CERN</a>) for $28.3 billion in cash.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="275"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="273"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-108" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-109" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">

</noscript>
</div>
</div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-6" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Justin Sullivan / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-110" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Long known for extravagant spending, Ellison has invested heavily in <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/articles/personal-finance/092414/investing-luxury-real-estate.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">luxury real estate</a> over the last decade. Perhaps his single most impressive acquisition was the $300 million purchase of nearly the entire Hawaiian island of Lanai in 2012, where the billionaire has lived since 2020. Ellison has built a hydroponics farm and a luxury spa on the island.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="276"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-111" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-112" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Ellison has focused his philanthropy on medical research. In 2016, he gave $200 million to the University of Southern California for a new cancer research center. Ellison backed the Oracle Team USA sailing team, which won the America&#39;s Cup racing series in 2010 and 2013.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="277"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-113" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-8-larry-page"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-114" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 8. Larry Page </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-115" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age:</strong> 49</li>
<li><strong>Residence: </strong>California</li>
<li><strong>Co-founder and Board Member:</strong> Alphabet (<a href="https://www.investopedia.com/markets/quote?tvwidgetsymbol=GOOG" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">GOOG</a>)</li>
<li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $88.8 billion</li>
<li><strong>Alphabet Ownership Stake:</strong> 6% ($74.8 billion total)</li>
<li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> $14 billion in cash<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="174"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-116" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-117" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Like several of the tech billionaires on this list, <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/articles/investing/081115/why-google-became-alphabet.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">Larry Page</a> embarked on his path to fame and fortune in a college dorm room. While attending Stanford University in 1995, Page and his friend Sergey Brin came up with the idea of&nbsp;improving&nbsp;Internet data extraction. The duo devised a new search engine technology they dubbed Backrub after its ability to assess links to a page.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-118" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-119" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
From there, Page and Brin went on to found Google in 1998, with Page serving as CEO of the company until 2001, and again between 2011 and 2019.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="152"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="79"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-120" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-121" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Google is the world&#39;s dominant Internet search engine, accounting for more than 92% of global search requests. In 2006, the company purchased YouTube, the top platform for user-submitted videos.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="200"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="160"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-122" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-123" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.9%;">
<img

<noscript>
<img

</noscript>
</div>
</div>
<figcaption id="mntl-figure-caption_1-0-7" class="comp figure-caption mntl-figure-caption figure-article-caption">
<span class="figure-article-caption-owner"><p>Justin Sullivan / Getty Images</p></span>
</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-124" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
After acquiring Android in 2005, Google released the Android mobile phone operating system in 2008. Google reorganized in 2015, becoming a <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/terms/s/subsidiary.asp" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">subsidiary</a> of Alphabet, a holding company.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="109"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="110"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="103"></span><br>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-125" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-126" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Page was among early investors in Planetary Resources, a space exploration and asteroid-mining company. Established in 2009, the company was acquired by blockchain firm ConsenSys in 2018 amid funding problems. He has also shown an interest in flying car companies, investing in both Kitty Hawk and Opener.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="111"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-127" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-128" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Shares of Google soared almost 50% in 2021, moving Page and Brin up the billionaire list. Page&#39;s net worth went from just below $52 billion in March 2020 to the current $86.9 billion.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="174"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="201"></span><br/>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-129" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-9-steve-ballmer"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-130" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 9. Steve Ballmer </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-131" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age: </strong>66</li><li><strong>Residence: </strong>Washington</li><li><strong>Owner:</strong> Los Angeles Clippers</li><li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $86.3 billion</li><li><strong>Microsoft Ownership Stake:</strong> 4% ($76.8 billion total)</li><li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> Los Angeles Clippers ($3.73 billion private asset), $5.73 billion in cash<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="279"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-132" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-133" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Steve Ballmer joined Microsoft in 1980 after Bill Gates convinced him to drop out of Stanford University&#39;s MBA program. He was Microsoft&#39;s 30th employee. Ballmer went on to succeed Gates as Microsoft CEO in 2000. He held the position until stepping down in 2014. Ballmer oversaw Microsoft&#39;s 2011 purchase of Skype for $8.5 billion.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="280"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-134" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-135" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Ballmer owns an estimated 4% of Microsoft, making him the software giant&#39;s largest individual shareholder. In 2014, shortly after stepping down as Microsoft CEO, Ballmer purchased the Los Angeles Clippers basketball team for $2 billion.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="279"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-136" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-137" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">
<div class="figure-media">
<div class="img-placeholder" style="padding-bottom:66.6%;">

<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-138" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Ballmer lived in the same dorm and on the same floor as Bill Gates while the two attended Harvard University. The brotherly relationship between the two became strained when Ballmer started pushing the tech company into hardware, such as the Surface tablet and the Windows mobile phone, during his tenure as CEO.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="281"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-139" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-10-carlos-slim"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-140" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> 10. Carlos Slim </span> </h2>
<ul id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-141" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
<li><strong>Age: </strong>82</li><li><strong>Residence: </strong>Mexico</li><li><strong>Owner:</strong> America Movil</li><li><strong>Net Worth:</strong> $85.7 billion</li><li><strong>America Movil Ownership Stake: </strong>Majority ($44.8 billion total)</li><li><strong>Other Assets:</strong> Cash ($7.98 billion), Inmuebles Carso ($5.38 billion), Grupo Carso ($9.18 billion), Grupo Financiero ($7.88 billion)<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="283"></span></li>
</ul>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-142" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-143" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
Carlos Slim derives the bulk of his wealth from his majority stake in America Movil, a telecommunications company based in Mexico City. He also has large stakes in the holding company Grupo Carso and the banking and insurance company Grupo Financiero. Additional holdings include many other publicly traded companies.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="283"></span>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-144" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<figure id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-145" class="comp mntl-sc-block-image inline-image mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-image mntl-sc-block-universal-image figure-landscape figure-high-res">

</figcaption>
</figure>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-146" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
A large portion of his stakes in these companies has been transferred to his six children and he has received billions of dollars in dividends from his holdings in the various public companies he has ownership in.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="283"></span><br/>
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-147" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-148" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-questionandanswer mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer">
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-who-are-the-top-10-richest-people-in-the-world"></span>
<h2 class="mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer__question">Who Are the Top 10 Richest People in the World?</h2>
<div class="mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer__answer"><p>The top 10 richest people in the world are:</p><ol><li>Bernard Arnault</li><li>Elon Musk</li><li>Jeff Bezos</li><li>Gautam Adani</li><li>Bill Gates<br/></li><li>Warren Buffett</li><li>Larry Ellison</li><li>Larry Page</li><li>Steve Ballmer</li><li>Carlos Slim</li></ol></div>
</div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-149" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-150" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-questionandanswer mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer">
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-who-is-the-worlds-richest-man-in-2023"></span>
<h2 class="mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer__question">Who Is the World&#39;s Richest Man in 2023?</h2>
<div class="mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer__answer"><p>As of January 2023, the world&#39;s richest man is Bernard Arnault, the co-founder, CEO, and chair of LVMH. He took over the top spot after Elon Musk&#39;s net worth dropped due to the declining value of Tesla&#39;s stock.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="278"></span></p></div>
</div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-151" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-152" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-questionandanswer mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer">
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-who-is-the-richest-woman-in-the-world"></span>
<h2 class="mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer__question">Who Is the Richest Woman in the World?</h2>
<div class="mntl-sc-block-questionandanswer__answer"><p>The richest woman in the world is Francoise Bettencourt Meyers. As of January 2023, her net worth is $82.8 billion. Her net worth is derived from her holdings in L&#39;Oreal, the world&#39;s largest cosmetics company.<span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="189"></span><span class="ql-inline-citation" data-cite="282"></span></p></div>
</div>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-153" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<span class="heading-toc" id="toc-the-bottom-line"></span> <h2 id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-154" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-heading mntl-sc-block-heading"> <span class="mntl-sc-block-heading__text"> The Bottom Line </span> </h2>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-155" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
If you want to get a little closer to making the richest billionaires rankings, you might&nbsp;need to become a technological innovator or luxury retail mastermind. Or you could <a href="https://www.investopedia.com/financial-edge/0412/the-everyday-lives-of-frugal-billionaires.aspx" data-component="link" data-source="inlineLink" data-type="internalLink" data-ordinal="1">keep it simple and focus on value investing</a>.
</p>
<div id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-156" class="comp mntl-sc-block mntl-sc-block-adslot mntl-block"></div>
<p id="mntl-sc-block_1-0-157" class="comp mntl-sc-block finance-sc-block-html mntl-sc-block-html">
It also wouldn’t hurt to have been born into wealth; however, the greatest fortunes on this list started as good ideas that people with creativity, drive, and connections used to build some of the world&#39;s largest companies.<br/>
</p>
</div>

><span class="link__wrapper">Ultra-High-Net-Worth Individual (UHNWI): Definition and Criteria</span></a>
<div id="related-terms__description_1-0-3" class="comp related-terms__description mntl-text-block">

<div id="related-terms__description_1-0-4" class="comp related-terms__description mntl-text-block">
